===============================================================================
 HARDWARE-ACCELERATED CODECS
===============================================================================

AGIF: enabled
FLAC: enabled
H263: disabled
H264: enabled
MJPA: enabled
MJPB: enabled
MJPG: enabled
MPG2: disabled
MPG4: disabled
MVC0: enabled
 PCM: enabled
THRA: enabled
VORB: enabled
 VP6: enabled
 VP8: enabled
WMV9: disabled
WVC1: disabled

Note 1: VP6, VP8, and MJPG are not handled by the hardware video decoder
in the Broadcom BCM2835 processor, but by the VideoCore GPU.  Enable these
by running:  sudo raspi-config -> Interfacing Options -> Camera -> Enable
or by adding "start_x=1" to /boot/config.txt

Note 2: GPU hardware-accelerated codecs will be disabled if "gpu_mem=16".
At least "gpu_mem=96" is required for the codecs to run correctly.

===============================================================================
 V4L2-CTL CODECS
===============================================================================

ioctl: VIDIOC_ENUM_FMT
	Type: Video Output Multiplanar

	[0]: 'H264' (H.264, compressed)
	[1]: 'MJPG' (Motion-JPEG, compressed)
	[2]: 'VP80' (VP8, compressed)

Note: The H.265 codec, new w/ the Pi 4B, isn't part of the videocore.
It's an entirely new block on the chip, so the VC6 knows nothing
about it.  Therefore, vcgencmd (which talks to the VC6) also knows
nothing about it.  The v4l2-ctl command used here, however, should
show the H.265 codec, when enabled, on the Pi 4B.

===============================================================================
 RSYSLOG.CONF ANALYSIS (***)
===============================================================================

This module creates a comprehensive listing of rsyslog.conf event logging.
The selector selects all messages of equal or higher severity.  For example,
news.err really means news.err, news.crit, news.alert, news.emerg.  And
mail,uucp.alert means mail.alert, mail.emerg, uucp.alert, and uucp.emerg.

Some versions of syslog allow an = character before the level specifier
(as in news.=err to act only on messages of that level.

The output below interprets the directives to show where things are going.
